H. Sri Kalki (G.I.) (FROF. M. T. NARASIMHIENGAR) To MALLESWARAM, BANGALORE. Date……………1931 DEAR SIR, I herewith send you for your acceptance and request you to kindly extend your liberal patronage to Our Publications of the Sacred Vedantic Series in several languages, for the Elevation and Salvation of all souls, irrespective of caste or creed, kind or sex, race or nation. It is estimated that at least Rs. 50,CCO are required to publish All My Works now on hand. Only very few devotees have kindly patronised these publications till now, to s cme extent.
